\subsection{Detailed Description}
This file contains all the types and functions that define the interface between a D\+RI driver and driver loader. Currently, the most common driver loader is the X\+Free86 lib\+G\+L.\+so. However, other loaders do exist, and in the future the server-\/side libglx.\+a will also be a loader.

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Kevin E. Martin \href{mailto:kevin@precisioninsight.com}{\tt kevin@precisioninsight.\+com} 

Ian Romanick \href{mailto:idr@us.ibm.com}{\tt idr@us.\+ibm.\+com} 

Kristian Høgsberg \href{mailto:krh@redhat.com}{\tt krh@redhat.\+com} 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

Existence of this extension means the driver can accept the {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+C\+T\+X\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+R\+O\+B\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+SS} flag and the {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+C\+T\+X\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+R\+I\+B\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+GY} attribute in {\ttfamily \hyperlink{struct_____d_r_idri2_extension_rec_acfac8ddb8a1248baf2e5863ea7132f11}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Idri2\+Extension\+Rec\+::create\+Context\+Attribs}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a4af74d002cfcc8c7915f9fbdbfa139e1}\label{dri__interface_8h_a4af74d002cfcc8c7915f9fbdbfa139e1}}

D\+RI config options extension.

This extension provides the X\+ML string containing driver options for use by the loader in supporting the driconf application. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_abc4e7f7031704022c639b85a4b9b10f7}\label{dri__interface_8h_abc4e7f7031704022c639b85a4b9b10f7}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS~\char`\"{}\+\_\+\+\_\+dri\+Driver\+Extensions\char`\"{}}

The remaining extensions describe driver extensions, immediately available interfaces provided by the driver. To start using the driver, dlsym() for the \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS symbol and look for the extension you need in the array. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a682e68eb31c1e6b9a8b6a641b8a2db96}\label{dri__interface_8h_a682e68eb31c1e6b9a8b6a641b8a2db96}} 
\index{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}!\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS}}
\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS}{\_\_DRI\_DRIVER\_GET\_EXTENSIONS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS~\char`\"{}\+\_\+\+\_\+dri\+Driver\+Get\+Extensions\char`\"{}}

This symbol replaces the \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+S\+I\+O\+NS symbol, and will be suffixed by \char`\"{}\+\_\+drivername\char`\"{}, allowing multiple drivers to be built into one library, and also giving the driver the chance to return a variable driver extensions struct depending on the driver name being loaded or any other system state.

The function prototype is\+:

const \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iextension $\ast$$\ast$\+\_\+\+\_\+dri\+Driver\+Get\+Extensions\+\_\+drivername(void); \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_ae6c1db358835b0e47eba79e2ddfd491b}\label{dri__interface_8h_ae6c1db358835b0e47eba79e2ddfd491b}}

\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+T\+A\+B\+LE@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+T\+A\+B\+LE}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+T\+A\+B\+LE}{\_\_DRI\_DRIVER\_VTABLE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+T\+A\+B\+LE~\char`\"{}D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+Driver\+Vtable\char`\"{}}

This extension provides a driver vtable to a set of common driver helper functions (dri\+Core\+Extension, dri\+D\+R\+I2\+Extension) within the driver implementation, as opposed to having to pass them through a global variable.

It is not intended to be public A\+PI to the actual loader, and the vtable layout may change at any time. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_ab1b772910a27d5142ba96445824ab46a}\label{dri__interface_8h_ab1b772910a27d5142ba96445824ab46a}}

\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+S\+\_\+\+R\+GB@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+S\+\_\+\+R\+GB}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+S\+\_\+\+R\+GB}{\_\_DRI\_IMAGE\_COMPONENTS\_RGB}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+S\+\_\+\+R\+GB~0x3001}

Queryable on images created by create\+Image\+From\+Names.

R\+GB and R\+G\+BA are may be usable directly as images but its still recommended to call from\+Planar with plane == 0.

Y\+\_\+\+U\+\_\+V, Y\+\_\+\+UV and Y\+\_\+\+X\+U\+XV all requires call to from\+Planar to create usable sub-\/images, sampling from images return raw Y\+UV data and color conversion needs to be done in the shader.

\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B565@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B565}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B565}{\_\_DRI\_IMAGE\_FORMAT\_RGB565}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B565~0x1001}

These formats correspond to the similarly named M\+E\+S\+A\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+$\ast$ tokens, except in the native endian of the C\+PU. For example, on little endian \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+X\+R\+G\+B8888 corresponds to M\+E\+S\+A\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+X\+R\+G\+B8888, but M\+E\+S\+A\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+X\+R\+G\+B8888\+\_\+\+R\+EV on big endian.

\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE is for images that aren\textquotesingle{}t directly usable by the driver (Y\+UV planar formats) but serve as a base image for creating sub-\/images for the different planes within the image.

R8, G\+R88 and N\+O\+NE should not be used with create\+Image\+Form\+Name or create\+Image, and are returned by query from sub images created with create\+Image\+From\+Names (N\+O\+NE, see above) and from\+Plane (R8 \& G\+R88). \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a287595100062804cac76dca4b36431c9}\label{dri__interface_8h_a287595100062804cac76dca4b36431c9}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+UP}{\_\_DRI\_IMAGE\_LOOKUP}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+UP~\char`\"{}D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+UP\char`\"{}}

This extension must be implemented by the loader and passed to the driver at screen creation time. The E\+G\+L\+Image entry points in the various client A\+P\+Is take opaque E\+G\+L\+Image handles and use this extension to map them to a \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iimage. At version 1, this extensions allows mapping E\+G\+L\+Image pointers to \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iimage pointers, but future versions could support other E\+G\+L\+Image-\/like, opaque types with new lookup functions. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a98fd54d68bd66a0e768862d5c6aeade0}\label{dri__interface_8h_a98fd54d68bd66a0e768862d5c6aeade0}}

\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+U\+P\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+U\+P\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}

\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+TE@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+TE}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+TE}{\_\_DRI\_USE\_INVALIDATE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+TE~\char`\"{}D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+Use\+Invalidate\char`\"{}}

Invalidate loader extension. The presence of this extension indicates to the D\+RI driver that the loader will call invalidate in the \+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I2\+\_\+\+F\+L\+U\+SH extension, whenever the needs to query for new buffers. This means that the D\+RI driver can drop the polling in \hyperlink{gl__mangle_8h_ab54b002beb984f066acd0dd7fff469dc}{gl\+Viewport()}.

The extension doesn\textquotesingle{}t provide any functionality, it\textquotesingle{}s only use to indicate to the driver that it can use the new semantics. A D\+RI driver can use this to switch between the different semantics or just refuse to initialize if this extension isn\textquotesingle{}t present. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_ab13c2c27e6c5c9005d6d6f1770acb056}\label{dri__interface_8h_ab13c2c27e6c5c9005d6d6f1770acb056}} 
\index{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}!\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}
\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}{\_\_DRI\_USE\_INVALIDATE\_VERSION}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a30777449fbcbb41d376496533cfe7907}\label{dri__interface_8h_a30777449fbcbb41d376496533cfe7907}} 
\index{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}!\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension}}
\index{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension@{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension}!dri\+\_\+interface.\+h@{dri\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension}{\_\_DRIgetDrawableInfoExtension}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \hyperlink{struct_____d_r_iget_drawable_info_extension_rec}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension\+Rec} \hyperlink{dri__interface_8h_a30777449fbcbb41d376496533cfe7907}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+D\+R\+Iget\+Drawable\+Info\+Extension}}

The following extensions describe loader features that the D\+RI driver can make use of. Some of these are mandatory, such as the get\+Drawable\+Info extension for D\+RI and the D\+RI Loader extensions for D\+R\+I2, while others are optional, and if present allow the driver to expose certain features. The loader pass in a N\+U\+LL terminated array of these extensions to the driver in the create\+New\+Screen constructor. \mbox{\Hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a37e0407153595dc88fe5d25127645cf1}\label{dri__interface_8h_a37e0407153595dc88fe5d25127645cf1}}
